<h3 class="s-post-summary--content-title">
<a class="s-link" href="/questions/79574963/using-nested-dynamic-arguments-in-custom-fmt-formatter">Using nested dynamic arguments in custom fmt formatter</a>
</h3>
<div class="s-post-summary--content-excerpt">
                Considering the following working example:
#include&lt;string&gt;
#include&lt;fmt/format.h&gt;
class foo_type{};
template&lt;&gt; struct fmt::formatter&lt;foo_type&gt;{
    private:
        std::...
            </div>
